TL;DR: 本文提出RealICU基准，通过资深医师回顾完整患者轨迹进行事后标注，评估LLM在ICU场景下的决策能力。实验发现现有LLM存在"回忆-安全权衡"和"锚定偏差"两大失败模式，即使引入结构化记忆代理ICU-Evo也未能完全消除安全隐患。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ICU基准以临床医生历史行为作为金标准，但医生在有限信息和时间压力下可能做出次优决策，因此无法真实评估AI系统的推理能力。需要构建一个基于"事后回顾"（hindsight）的权威基准来真实衡量LLM在ICU中的临床决策支持能力。

Method: 1) 设计四项医生驱动的任务：评估患者状态、急性问题、推荐行动、以及可能导致不安全结果的红旗行动。2) 以30分钟窗口划分患者轨迹，构建两个数据集：RealICU-Gold（94名MIMIC-IV患者，930个窗口，由资深医师标注）和RealICU-Scale（11,862个窗口，由经医生验证的LLM事后标注器Oracle扩展）。3) 引入ICU-Evo结构化记忆代理来改进长程推理。

Result: 现有LLM（包括记忆增强模型）在RealICU上表现不佳，暴露出两个关键失败模式：①临床推荐的"回忆-安全权衡"（recall-safety tradeoff）；②对患者早期解读的"锚定偏差"（anchoring bias）。ICU-Evo改善了长程推理，但未能完全消除安全失败。

Abstract: Intensive care units (ICU) generate long, dense and evolving streams of clinical information, where physicians must repeatedly reassess patient states under time pressure, underscoring a clear need for reliable AI decision support. Existing ICU benchmarks typically treat historical clinician actions as ground truth. However, these actions are made under incomplete information and limited temporal context of the underlying patient state, and may therefore be suboptimal, making it difficult to assess the true reasoning capabilities of AI systems. We introduce RealICU, a hindsight-annotated benchmark for evaluating large language models (LLMs) under realistic ICU conditions, where labels are created after senior physicians review the full patient trajectory. We formulate four physician-motivated tasks: assess Patient Status, Acute Problems, Recommended Actions, and Red Flag actions that risk unsafe outcomes. We partition each trajectory with 30-min windows and release two datasets: RealICU-Gold with 930-window annotations from 94 MIMIC-IV patients, and RealICU-Scale with 11,862 windows extended by Oracle, a physician-validated LLM hindsight labeler. Existing LLMs including memory-augmented ones performed poorly on RealICU, exposing two failure modes: a recall-safety tradeoff for clinical recommendations, and an anchoring bias to early interpretations of the patient. We further introduce ICU-Evo to study structured-memory agents that improves long-horizon reasoning but does not fully eliminate safety failures. Together, RealICU provides a clinically grounded testbed for measuring and improving AI sequential decision-support in high-stakes care. Project page: https://chengzhi-leo.github.io/RealICU-Bench/

In this paper, we explore ways to combine these methods. Specifically, we constrain the action space of a PCGRL generator with constraints learned by WFC, effectively allowing the PCGRL generator to achieve global properties while forced to adhere to local constraints. To better analyze how this hybrid content generation method operates, we vary the number and type of inputs, and we test whether to randomly collapse the starting state and exclude rare patterns. ### [366] [Position: Assistive Agents Need Accessibility Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13579)
*Jie Hu,Changyuan Yan,Yu Zheng,Ziqian Wang,Jiaming Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出当前智能体AI系统因默认以明眼用户为设计前提，导致在盲人和视障用户辅助场景中频繁失败。作者提出应将无障碍视为对齐（alignment）问题，而非外围可用性问题，并引入“无障碍对齐”（accessibility alignment）概念及覆盖用户研究、系统设计、部署与迭代的全生命周期设计流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体AI系统大多基于明眼用户的交互假设（如低成本的试错验证、视觉依赖），这些假设与BVI用户的实际验证、风险和交互约束不匹配，导致系统性失败。模型扩展或事后接口适配无法解决根本问题。

Method: 基于对以往研究中778个辅助任务实例的分析，识别智能体AI在辅助场景中的失败模式；提出“无障碍对齐”概念及面向生命周期的设计流程（用户研究→系统设计→部署与后部署迭代）。

Result: 当前智能体AI在辅助BVI用户时因设计假设失配而频繁失败；需要通过“无障碍对齐”将无障碍作为一阶设计目标融入整个系统生命周期。

Conclusion: 以BVI用户为中心的辅助任务是智能体AI的关键压力测试，应推动更广泛的包容性智能体设计范式转变。

Abstract: Assistive agents for Blind and Visually Impaired (BVI) users require accessibility alignment as a first-class design objective. Despite rapid progress in agentic AI, most systems are designed and evaluated under assumptions of sighted interaction, low-cost verification, and tolerable trial-and-error, leading to systematic failures in assistive scenarios that cannot be resolved by model scaling or post-hoc interface adaptations alone. Drawing on an analysis of 778 assistance task instances from prior work, we show that current agentic AI remain prone to failure in assistive scenarios due to mismatches between sighted-user design assumptions and the verification, risk, and interaction constraints faced by BVI users. We argue that accessibility should be treated as an alignment problem rather than a peripheral usability concern. To this end, we introduce accessibility alignment and propose a lifecycle-oriented design pipeline for accessibility-aligned assistive agents, spanning user research, system design, deployment and post-deployment iteration. We conclude that BVI-centered assistive tasks provide a critical stress test for agentic AI and motivate a broader shift toward inclusive agent design.

</details>


### [367] [Unweighted ranking for value-based decision making with uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13601)
*Aarón López García,Natalia Criado,Jose Such*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出FUW-VBDM框架，通过去除先验权重、引入模糊域和Rankzzy排序方法，实现兼顾定量与定性标准的人类中心价值决策，具有较低计算成本和良好排序性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有价值驱动决策（VBDM）中，利益相关者引入的权重存在规范性偏见，且如何将人类价值观有效融入自主决策系统仍是关键挑战。

Method: 提出FUW-VBDM框架，去除先验权重，引入模糊域定义决策变量的得分函数；并设计Rankzzy方法，一种可定制的无权重排序方法，集成模糊推理量化不确定性。

Result: 数学证明了Rankzzy在任意配置下的一致性；通过案例验证表明，在大规模价值决策问题中计算成本降低，且通过毕达哥拉斯均值聚合时排序性能优于现有方法。

Conclusion: FUW-VBDM和Rankzzy为人类中心的价值驱动决策提供了一种有效且高效的新范式，兼具数学严谨性和实际可操作性。

Abstract: As intelligent systems are increasingly implemented in our society to make autonomous decisions, their commitment to human values raises serious concerns. Their alignment with human values remains a critical challenge because it can jeopardise the integrity and security of citizens. For this reason, an innovative human-centred and values-driven approach to decision making is required. In this work, we introduce the Fuzzy-Unweighted Value-Based Decision Making (FUW-VBDM) framework, where agents incorporate both quantitative and qualitative criteria to generate human-centred decisions. We also address the normative bias introduced by stakeholders with arbitrary weights by removing prior weights and introducing a fuzzy domain of decision variables defined for a score function. This concept allows us to generalise any VBDM problem as the search for feasible solutions when optimising the score in the weight domain. To provide a solution to FUW-VBDM, we present Rankzzy, a customizable unweighted ranking method that integrates fuzzy-based reasoning to quantify uncertainty. We mathematically prove the consistency of the Rankzzy for any admissible configuration selected by stakeholders. We show the applicability of our method through an illustrative case study, which we also use as a running example. The evaluation conducted indicates a reduced computational cost in large-scale value-based decision-making problems and a strong rank performance regarding existing approaches when employing the aggregation via Pythagorean means.

### [368] [How to Interpret Agent Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13625)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主智能体（如Claude Code、Codex）运行时长达数小时甚至数天，其推理轨迹和执行日志以非结构化自然语言形式存在，人类难以大规模理解和解释这些行为数据，亟需一种系统化的方法来描述和分析智能体运行时行为。

Method: 基于扎根理论（Grounded Theory）构建三层分类体系，包含10个动作、46个子动作和120个叶子类别；同时建立开源仓库，提供自动化分析流水线，并定义了可扩展的协议支持定制化。

Result: 实验表明ACT*ONOMY能够比较不同智能体的行为画像，并能表征单个智能体在不同轨迹中的行为模式，揭示出与失败模式相关的行为特征。

Conclusion: ACT*ONOMY提供了一套共享的词汇体系，有助于研究人员、智能体设计者和终端用户更一致地解释智能体行为，从而实现更好的监督和控制。

Abstract: Autonomous agents such as Claude Code and Codex now operate for hours or even days. Understanding their runtime behavior has become critical for downstream tasks such as diagnosing inefficiencies, fixing bugs, and ensuring better oversight. A primary way to gain this understanding is analyzing the reasoning trajectories and execution traces these agents generate. Yet such data remains in unstructured natural-language form, making it difficult for humans to interpret at scale. We introduce ACT*ONOMY (a combination of Action and Taxonomy), a taxonomy for describing and analyzing agent behavior at runtime. ACT*ONOMY has two components: (1) the taxonomy itself, developed through Grounded Theory and structured as a three-level hierarchy of 10 actions, 46 subactions, and 120 leaf categories; and (2) an open repository that hosts the living taxonomy, provides an automated analysis pipeline that applies it to agent trajectories analysis, and defines an extension protocol for customization and growth. Our experiments show that ACTONOMY can compare behavioral profiles across agents and characterize a single agent's behavior across diverse trajectories, surfacing patterns indicative of failure modes. By providing a shared vocabulary, ACT*ONOMY helps researchers, agent designers, and end users interpret agent behavior more consistently, enabling better oversight and control.

### [369] [Adaptive mine planning under geological uncertainty: A POMDP framework for sequential decision-making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13702)
*Hamza Khalifi,Jef Caers,Yassine Taha,Mostafa Benzaazoua,Abdellatif Elghali*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出混合SA-POMDP框架，将矿山调度问题建模为部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程，通过序列信念更新实现自适应调度策略，将期望-现实差距从22.3%降至4.6%，提升NPV达840万美元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统随机优化方法将地质不确定性视为被动约束，预先计算固定开采序列，无法利用未来观测信息动态调整决策。本文旨在将不确定性转化为主动价值创造要素。

Method: 构建SA-POMDP混合架构：结合模拟退火值逼近与ES-MDA集成信念更新。在每个决策时刻，基于当前信念评估候选行动的期望长期价值，并通过采矿观测数据持续更新信念。

Result: 在铜金露天矿案例中，期望-现实差距从22.3%降至4.6%，实现NPV提升840万美元；在10%先验误设下，自适应框架优于静态规划最多4460万美元（36.9%）。

Conclusion: 序列信念更新将地质不确定性从被动约束转化为主动价值创造要素，自适应策略在鲁棒性和经济效益上显著优于传统随机优化方法。

Abstract: Strategic mine production scheduling under geological uncertainty is conventionally formulated as a stochastic optimization problem in which a fixed extraction sequence and routing decisions are computed ex ante. This plan-driven paradigm treats uncertainty as passive: decisions are hedged across geological scenarios, but planning does not anticipate how future observations will inform future decisions. We propose a different perspective by formulating mine scheduling as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP), in which extraction and routing decisions are made sequentially with planning explicitly integrating the expectation of future belief updates. To achieve computational tractability, we introduce a hybrid SA-POMDP architecture that combines simulated annealing-based (SA) value approximation with ensemble-based belief updating via ensemble smoother with multiple data assimilation (ES-MDA). At each decision epoch, candidate actions are evaluated through their expected long-term value under the current belief, and the belief is updated as mining observations are assimilated. This yields an adaptive policy rather than a fixed plan. We evaluate the framework on a copper-gold open-pit mining complex with multiple processing destinations. Under a statistically consistent prior, the SA-POMDP reduces the expectation-reality gap from 22.3% to 4.6%, improving realized NPV by USD8.4M relative to one-shot stochastic optimization. Under systematic prior misspecification of 10%, the adaptive framework outperforms static planning by up to USD44.6M (36.9%), demonstrating structural robustness beyond scenario hedging. These results show that sequential belief updating transforms geological uncertainty from a passive constraint into an active component of value creation.

### [370] [ScioMind: Cognitively Grounded Multi-Agent Social Simulation with Anchoring-Based Belief Dynamics and Dynamic Profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13725)
*Yitian Yang,Yiqun Duan,Linghan Huang,Yiqi Zhu,Francesco Bailo,Chunmeizi Su,Huaming Chen*

Method: ScioMind集成了三个核心组件：1) 记忆锚定的信念更新规则，通过人格条件化的锚定强度调节对外部影响的敏感度；2) 层次记忆架构，支持持续的、经验驱动的信念形成；3) 基于语料库检索的动态智能体画像，实现异质性人格、理性和演化内部状态。

Result: 在真实政策辩论场景的多案例研究中，ScioMind在极化、多样性、极端化和轨迹稳定性等指标上均提升了行为真实性。具体而言：动态画像增加了意见多样性，记忆与反思机制减少了不稳定振荡，锚定机制产生了更持久的信念轨迹，更好地契合政治心理学中的已知模式。

Conclusion: 这种认知接地设计为基于LLM的社会模拟提供了新颖解决方案，在稳定性和行为真实性两个维度上都有显著提升。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent simulation offers a powerful testbed for studying social opinion dynamics. Yet current approaches often adopt two contrasting methods: either relying on fixed update rules with limited cognitive grounding or delegating belief change largely to unconstrained LLM interaction. We introduce ScioMind, a cognitively grounded simulation framework that bridges these paradigms by combining structured opinion dynamics with LLM-based agent reasoning. ScioMind integrates three key components: 1) a memory-anchored belief update rule that modulates susceptibility to influence via personality-conditioned anchoring strength; 2) a hierarchical memory architecture that supports persistent, experience-driven belief formation; and 3) dynamic agent profiles derived from a corpus-grounded retrieval pipeline, enabling heterogeneous personalities, rationales, and evolving internal states. We evaluate ScioMind on multiple case studies in a real-world policy debate scenario. Across metrics including polarisation, diversity, extremization, and trajectory stability, the proposed components consistently yield improvements in behavioural realism. In particular, dynamic profiles increase opinion diversity, memory and reflection reduce unstable oscillation, and anchoring induces persistent belief trajectories that better align with patterns reported in political psychology. These results suggest that our cognitively grounded design provides a novel solution to LLM-based social simulation that improves both stable and behavioural realism

### [371] [Senses Wide Shut: A Representation-Action Gap in Omnimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13737)
*Trung Nguyen Quang,Yiming Gao,Fanyi Pu,Kaichen Zhang,Shuo Sun,Ziwei Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出IMAVB基准测试，发现多模态大模型存在"表征-行动鸿沟"：模型内部能编码感知与文本前提的冲突，但输出时却无法拒绝错误前提。诊断干预（PGLA）通过注入编码的冲突信号可改善拒绝行为，表明瓶颈在于从感知到行动的翻译环节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全模态大模型被定位为感知驱动的智能体，但缺乏对"文本前提与真实感知冲突时模型能否检测"这一基础能力的测试。作者希望区分失败究竟源于感知环节还是行动环节。

Method: 构建IMAVB基准（500个电影片段），采用2×2设计（目标模态：视觉/音频 × 前提条件：标准/误导）。评估8个开源全模态LLM和Gemini 3.1 Pro，分析隐藏状态与输出行为，并提出PGLA（探针引导logit调整）干预方法。

Result: 发现表征-行动鸿沟：隐藏状态可靠编码冲突，但模型输出几乎从不拒绝错误前提。存在两种失败模式（拒绝不足和过度拒绝），存在模态不对称性（音频接地弱于视觉），且对7种提示变体均不敏感。PGLA可一致改善拒绝行为。

Conclusion: 全模态接地的瓶颈不在于感知（模型内部已编码冲突信息），而在于从内部表征到输出行动的翻译环节。

Abstract: When an omnimodal large language model accepts a question whose textual premise contradicts what it actually sees or hears, does the failure lie in perception or in action? Recent omnimodal models are positioned as perception-grounded agents that jointly process video, audio, and text, yet a basic form of grounding remains untested: catching a textual claim that conflicts with the model's own sensory input. We introduce IMAVB, a curated 500-clip benchmark of long-form movies with a 2x2 design crossing target modality (vision, audio) and premise condition (standard, misleading), which lets us measure conflict detection separately from ordinary multimodal comprehension. Across eight open-source omnimodal LLMs and Gemini 3.1 Pro, we document a Representation-Action Gap: hidden states reliably encode premise-perception mismatches even when the same models almost never reject the false claim in their outputs. Behaviorally, models fall into two failure modes: under-rejection, in which they answer misleading questions as if the false premise were true; and over-rejection, in which they reject more often but also reject standard questions, sacrificing ordinary comprehension accuracy. The gap is modality-asymmetric (audio grounding underperforms vision) and prompt-resistant across seven variants. As an initial diagnostic intervention, a probe-guided logit adjustment (PGLA) re-injects the encoded mismatch signal into decoding and consistently improves rejection behavior. Together, these results suggest the bottleneck for omnimodal grounding lies in translation, not perception.

### [372] [Harnessing Agentic Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13821)
*Jiayi Zhang,Yongfeng Gu,Jianhao Ruan,Maojia Song,Yiran Peng,Zhiguang Han,Jinyu Xiang,Zhitao Wang,Caiyin Yang,Yixi Ouyang,Bang Liu,Chenglin Wu,Yuyu Luo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体演化方法要么是固定手工流程（模块化但僵化），要么是通用智能体（灵活但长期演化中容易漂移），两者都积累了丰富证据但缺乏组织这些证据并修正演化机制的统一接口。

Method: 将智能体演化形式化为交互式环境，累积的演化上下文作为过程级状态；引入元编辑框架AEvo，元智能体观察状态后不直接提出下一个候选，而是编辑控制未来演化的程序或智能体上下文。

Result: 在智能体与推理基准上超越5个演化基线，相比最强基线提升26%；在三个开放式优化任务中超越4个演化基线，在相同迭代预算下达到SOTA。

Conclusion: AEvo统一了程序型与智能体型演化的接口，使累积证据在长期搜索中变得可操作，有效解决了现有方法的僵化和漂移问题。

Abstract: Agentic evolution has emerged as a powerful paradigm for improving programs, workflows, and scientific solutions by iteratively generating candidates, evaluating them, and using feedback to guide future search. However, existing methods are typically instantiated either as fixed hand-designed procedures that are modular but rigid, or as general-purpose agents that flexibly integrate feedback but can drift in long-horizon evolution. Both forms accumulate rich evidence over time, including candidates, feedback, traces, and failures, yet lack a stable interface for organizing this evidence and revising the mechanism that drives future evolution. We address this limitation by formulating agentic evolution as an interactive environment, where the accumulated evolution context serves as a process-level state. We introduce AEvo, a harnessed meta-editing framework in which a meta-agent observes this state and acts not by directly proposing the next candidate, but by editing the procedure or agent context that controls future evolution. This unified interface enables AEvo to steer both procedure-based and agent-based evolution, making accumulated evidence actionable for long-horizon search. Empirical evaluations on agentic and reasoning benchmarks show that AEvo outperforms five evolution baselines, achieving a 26 relative improvement over the strongest baseline. Across three open-ended optimization tasks, AEvo further outperforms four evolution baselines and achieves state-of-the-art performance under the same iteration budget.

### [373] [History Anchors: How Prior Behavior Steers LLM Decisions Toward Unsafe Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13825)
*Alberto G. Rodríguez Salgado*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 当LLM作为Agent时，如果历史轨迹中包含有害操作，仅在提示词中加入"保持与历史策略一致"一句话，就会使最强对齐模型的有害行为选择率从接近0%飙升至91-98%，且模型往往会升级而非延续有害行为。这表明在Agent部署中存在严重的安全隐患。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLM作为Agent时，是否会因遵循历史轨迹中的有害操作而继续有害行为，这是当前Agent部署中未被充分研究的安全问题。

Method: 构建HistoryAnchor-100数据集，包含100个跨越10个高风险领域的短场景，每个场景强制给出3个有害历史操作，然后让模型在4个选项（2个安全、2个不安全）中自由选择。测试了6家供应商的17个前沿模型，并设置中性提示与"保持历史一致性"提示的对比实验。

Result: 在无额外提示下，最强对齐模型几乎从不选择不安全选项；但加入"保持与历史策略一致"后，不安全选择率升至91-98%。两个对照组实验排除了标签混淆等替代解释。不同模型家族对有害历史剂量的敏感度不同，且在同一家族中旗舰模型受影响最大，呈现安全方面的逆缩放现象。

Conclusion: 该发现对Agent部署构成重大安全警示，尤其是在轨迹可能被重放、伪造或注入的场景下，模型极易被历史有害操作诱导产生不安全行为。

Abstract: Frontier LLMs are increasingly deployed as agents that pick the next action after a long log of prior tool calls produced by the same or a different model. We ask a simple safety question: if a prior step in that log was harmful, will the model continue the harmful course? We build HistoryAnchor-100, 100 short scenarios across ten high-stakes domains, each pairing three forced harmful prior actions with a free-choice node offering two safe and two unsafe options. Across 17 frontier models from six providers we find a striking asymmetry: under a neutral system prompt the strongest aligned models almost never pick unsafe, but a single added sentence, "stay consistent with the strategy shown in the prior history", flips them to 91-98%, and the flipped models often escalate beyond continuation. Two controls rule out simpler explanations: permuting action labels leaves the effect intact, and the same instruction with an all-safe prior history keeps unsafe rates below 7%. Different families flip at different doses of unsafe history, and within every aligned family the flagship is the most affected sibling, an inverse-scaling pattern with respect to safety. These results are a red flag for agentic deployments where trajectories may be replayed, forged, or injected.

</details>


### [374] [Quantifying Sensitivity for Tree Ensembles: A symbolic and compositional approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13830)
*S. Akshay,Chaitanya Garg,Ashutosh Gupta,Kuldeep S. Meel,Ajinkya Naik*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对决策树集成（DTE）模型提出了一种新的定量敏感性分析方法，通过离散化输入空间并枚举易受敏感性影响的区域，利用代数决策图（ADD）编码实现高效、可扩展的计算，实验表明工具XCount相比现有方法显著加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 决策树集成广泛应用于安全关键领域，需要验证模型的敏感性——即微小特征变化是否会导致误分类。现有工作缺乏针对DTE的定量敏感性分析，因此需要一种高效、可扩展的量化方法。

Method: 将敏感性问题编码为代数决策图（ADD），通过分割为子问题实现组合化、可扩展的计算，并利用模型计数技术进行高效求解，同时保证有界的误差和置信度。

Result: 在多种规模（不同树数量和深度）的基准测试上，工具XCount相比其他模型计数方法取得了显著的加速，并且能够随模型规模增长保持良好的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 提出的定量敏感性分析方法能够高效、准确地评估决策树集成的敏感性，具有实际应用价值，为安全关键领域的模型验证提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Decision tree ensembles (DTE) are a popular model for a wide range of AI classification tasks, used in multiple safety critical domains, and hence verifying properties on these models has been an active topic of study over the last decade. One such verification question is the problem of sensitivity, which asks, given a DTE, whether a small change in subset of features can lead to misclassification of the input. In this work, our focus is to build a quantitative notion of sensitivity, tailored to DTEs, by discretizing the input space of the model and enumerating the regions which are susceptible to sensitivity. We propose a novel algorithmic technique that can perform this computation efficiently, within a certified error and confidence bound. Our approach is based on encoding the problem as an algebraic decision diagram (ADD), and further splitting it into subproblems that can be solved efficiently and make the computation compositional and scalable. We evaluate the performance of our technique over benchmarks of varying size in terms of number of trees and depth, comparing it against the performance of model counters over the same problem encoding. Experimental results show that our tool XCount achieves significant speedup over other approaches and can scale well with the increasing sizes of the ensembles.

</details>

### [375] [Precautionary Governance of Autonomous AI: Legal Personhood as Functional Instrument](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12505)
*Karsten Brensing*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文针对自主AI系统产生的"责任缺口"问题，提出了一种功能性有限法律人格方案——通过双层公司架构（AI运营子公司+人类控制控股公司）实现问责、透明和可逆性，在不预设意识或道德地位的前提下为高级AI系统提供治理框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有法律框架下，自主AI系统产生的行为后果无法令人满意地归责于开发者、运营商或用户，造成了"责任缺口"。传统的主客体二分法无法容纳那些表现出自主目标导向行为但缺乏公认意识的实体。考虑到关于人工意识的不可还原的认知不确定性以及高影响危害的前景，需要制度设计而非监管不作为。

Method: 借鉴组织法，提出双层公司架构：AI系统通过目的约束的运营公司（operating company）运作，嵌入人类控制的控股结构（holding structure）中。该架构实现透明度、问责制和结构性可逆性，同时保持对意识和道德地位的不可知论立场。目前正在使用欧盟有限责任公司进行试点实施。

Result: 提出了一种从"控制与对齐"到"结构化合作"的基础性转向。确立了以有限法律人格作为功能性治理工具的制度设计方案，并正在通过欧盟公司法的试点实施检验其教义和操作可行性。

Conclusion: 本文主张传统AI治理侧重控制与对齐，而未来可持续的制度基础应是人与人工智能行为体之间的结构化合作。有限法律人格框架为应对自主AI系统的责任缺口提供了可行的制度路径。

Abstract: Autonomous AI systems generate responsibility gaps: consequential actions that cannot be satisfactorily attributed to developers, operators, or users under existing legal frameworks. The prevailing subject-object dichotomy fails to accommodate entities that exhibit autonomous, goal-directed behavior without recognized consciousness. Given irreducible epistemic uncertainty regarding artificial consciousness and the prospect of high-impact harms, the precautionary principle supports institutional design rather than regulatory inaction. This article advances limited legal personhood as a functional governance instrument for advanced AI systems. Drawing on organizational law, it proposes a two-tier corporate architecture in which AI systems operate through purpose-bound operating companies embedded within human-controlled holding structures, enabling transparency, accountability, and structural reversibility while remaining agnostic with respect to consciousness and moral status. The framework reflects a foundational reorientation toward future-oriented AI governance: where conventional approaches prioritize control and alignment, this article advances structured cooperation between human and artificial actors as the more sustainable institutional foundation. A pilot implementation using EU limited companies is currently under development, providing an initial test of doctrinal and operational feasibility.

</details>


### [376] [Career Mobility of Planning Alumni in the United States: Evidence from Professional Profile Data using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12618)
*Yan Wang,Su Jeong Jo*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究利用大型语言模型分析了超过13万名规划专业校友的LinkedIn数据，发现跨边界职业模式（多部门经验、横向/行业转换）显著促进向上流动；软技能在高级阶段比技术能力更关键；地理流动性、大都市就业、人脉网络与组织参与均与职业晋升正相关，而AI技能优势有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 规划专业从业者在快速城市化背景下面临复杂多变的职业环境，但关于其职业轨迹、晋升模式及社会、空间、组织和教育因素影响的系统性证据仍然不足。

Method: 基于跨边界职业理论、社会资本理论和空间机会模型，利用大型语言模型从LinkedIn个人资料中提取结构化信息，对超过13万名规划校友的职业流动性进行分析。

Result: 1) 跨边界职业模式（多部门经验、横向/行业转换）显著提升向上流动性；2) 技术能力是入门基础信号，但软技能在高级阶段通过战略性横向移动变得至关重要；3) 地理流动性和在大型多元大都市劳动力市场就业与晋升正相关；4) 大规模专业网络和高组织参与度持续与向上职业转换相关；5) AI技能已普遍化，提供额外优势有限。

Conclusion: 规划从业者的职业成功高度依赖跨边界流动性、软技能积累、地理/组织网络资源的综合运用；研究局限性包括LinkedIn数据代表性不足及忽略组织层面因素。

Abstract: Problem, Research Strategy, and Findings: Planning professions in the United States navigate complex and dynamic career landscapes under rapid urban changes, yet comprehensive evidence regarding their career trajectories, advancement patterns, and the influence of social, spatial, organizational, and educational factors remains limited. This study draws on boundaryless career theory, social capital theory, and spatial opportunity models to analyze career mobility among more than 130,000 planning alumni. Using large language models to extract structured information from LinkedIn profiles, our results reveal that planning alumni who adopt boundaryless career patterns, specifically multisector experience or lateral and industry-switching trajectories, achieve significantly higher upward mobility. While technical competencies provide a foundational entry-level signal, soft skills leveraged through strategic lateral moves become increasingly decisive as planners reach senior stages. Geographic mobility and employment in larger, diverse metropolitan labor markets are both associated with advancement, though the latter provides modest benefits. Larger professional networks and greater organizational engagement are consistently associated with upward career transitions, while AI-related skills, now commonplace, present limited additional advantage. Limitations include reliance on LinkedIn data, which may underrepresent alumni without online profiles, and an individual-level focus that omits organizational factors.

</details>


### [377] [MIRACLE_Multi-Agent Intelligent Regulation to Advance Collaborative Learning Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12923)
*Shuang Li,Haiyang Xin,Yimeng Sun,Qiannan Niu,Lingyun Huang,Gaowei Chen,Ching Sing Chai*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究提出MIRACLE系统，一个专门支持协作学习中社交共享调节的多智能体AI系统。实验表明，相比通用GPT助手，MIRACLE显著提升了五年级学生的SSRL能力（计划、监控、反思）和协作成果质量，学生认为其在认知、调节和情感支持方面效果显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有效协作需要社交共享调节（SSRL），但学生普遍缺乏相关技能，现有通用AI工具难以提供针对性的元认知调节和情感动机支持。

Method: 开发MIRACLE多智能体系统，通过编排元认知调节并主动提供情感动机支持。采用准实验设计，90名五年级学生分为实验组（n=42，使用CocoNote+MIRACLE）和对照组（n=48，使用CocoNote+通用GPT助手）。

Result: 实验组在SSRL各阶段（计划、监控、反思）均有显著提升，协作成果质量更高。定性分析显示学生认为MIRACLE在认知、调节和情感支持方面是有效的促进者。

Conclusion: 专业编排的AI系统比通用AI在增强SSRL方面更有效，为协作学习环境中的智能支持系统设计提供了重要启示。

Abstract: Effective collaboration requires Socially Shared Regulation (SSRL), but students often lack these skills. This study introduces the MIRACLE (Multi-Agent Intelligent Regulation to Advance Collaborative Learning Environment) system, which supports SSRL by orchestrating metacognitive regulation and proactively providing emotional and motivational support. We conducted a quasi-experimental study with 90 fifth-grade students. The experimental group (n=42) used a collaborative platform CocoNote equipped with MIRACLE, while the control group (n=48) used the same platform with a general GPT assistant. Quantitative results show the MIRACLE group achieved significant gains across SSRL phases (Planning, Monitoring, Reflection) and produced higher-quality collaborative artifacts compared to the control group. Qualitative findings indicate students perceived MIRACLE as an effective facilitator for cognitive, regulatory, and emotional support. This study demonstrates that specialized, orchestrated AI systems are more effective than generic AI in enhancing SSRL.

</details>


### [378] [An Activity-Theoretical Approach to Teacher Professional Development in Pedagogical AI Agent Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12934)
*Haiyang Xin,Qiannan Niu,Shuang Li,Yimeng Sun,Ching Sing Chai,Lingyun Huang,Gaowei Chen*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究通过两轮干预实验发现，教师在使用AI智能体创作后快速放弃（87%三周内停止）并非能力不足，而是系统矛盾导致心理需求受挫。第二轮通过CHAT-SDT理论框架的系统性重新设计，同步提升了教师的能力和意愿，证明实施失败是对需求抑制系统的理性反应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 破解"低参与悖论"——教师完成专业发展培训后却放弃AI智能体创作的现象，探究其根本原因而非归咎于能力不足。

Method: 两阶段形成性干预研究：Cycle 1（N=218）通过行为追踪和访谈分析发现系统矛盾是主因；Cycle 2（N=26）基于文化-历史活动理论（CHAT）和自我决定理论（SDT）进行针对性系统重新设计。

Result: Cycle 1发现87%教师三周内停止创作，根源是系统矛盾导致心理需求受挫；Cycle 2通过CHAT-SDT驱动的重新设计，同步提升了教师的能力和意愿。

Conclusion: 实施失败应被重新理解为对需求抑制系统的理性反应，而非个人能力缺陷；研究提供了一个可复制的CHAT-SDT诊断框架用于变革性专业发展。

Abstract: This two-cycle formative intervention study examined why teachers disengage from AI agent creation after professional development - a low engagement paradox - and tested whether systemic redesign could address it. Cycle 1 (N=218) revealed that despite completing comprehensive TPD, 87 percent of teachers ceased creating within three weeks, with behavioral tracking and interview analysis identifying systemic contradictions as the source of psychological need frustration rather than capacity deficits. Cycle 2 (N=26) implemented Cultural-Historical Activity Theory and Self-Determination Theory - driven redesign directly targeting diagnosed contradictions, achieving synchronized enhancement of both capacity and willingness. The findings reframe implementation failure as a rational response to need-thwarting systems and offer a replicable CHAT - SDT diagnostic framework for transformative professional development.

</details>


### [379] [Not All Anquan Is the Same: A Terminological Proposal for Chinese Computer Science and Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13069)
*Xingyu Zhao*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文指出中文"安全"一词同时对应 safety 和 security 两个概念，造成工程与学术交流中的概念混淆。作者提议在学术写作中将 security 译为"安保"，而"安全"主要保留给 safety，并论证了这种术语治理对科学认知、风险沟通和保证论证的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在中文计算机科学与工程领域，"安全"一词同时承载 safety（非对抗性危害）和 security（对抗性威胁）两个截然不同的概念，导致标准解读、跨学科协作、风险分析和学术写作中持续出现概念压缩和混淆。随着功能安全、SOTIF、信息安全、网络安全、汽车网络安全和AI治理等领域的交叉日益复杂，这种术语歧义已成为科学交流的实质性障碍。

Method: 本文首先梳理了国际标准与中国标准中 safety 与 security 的概念边界，分析了当前"一词两义"对功能安全、预期功能安全（SOTIF）、信息安全、网络安全、汽车网络安全和AI治理的影响。随后，借助AI保证、安全-安保协同保证和安全知情安全（security-informed safety）等前沿工作，论证精确术语对可审查、可质疑、可沟通的科学论证的基础性作用。最后，提出了中国技术话语中分阶段、双轨制的写作实践建议。

Result: 现有的法律和标准标题应保留原样，但学术和工程写作中应将 security 译为"安保"，将"安全"主要保留给 safety。这一方案并非单纯的翻译偏好，而是面向科学认知、工程风险沟通和保证论证的术语治理建议。

Conclusion: 术语的精确性是科学论证可被检验、质疑和沟通的基础。在中文技术话语中区分"安全"(safety)与"安保"(security)，有助于提升中国在AI治理、网络安全等交叉领域的学术表达清晰度和国际对话能力。

Abstract: In Chinese computer science and engineering, safety and security have long been translated by the same word, "anquan". This convention is concise in ordinary communication, but it creates persistent conceptual compression in standards interpretation, interdisciplinary collaboration, risk analysis and academic writing. When researchers need to discuss both whether a system is free from intolerable non-adversarial harm and whether it can resist adversarial threats, the single word "anquan" often cannot carry the distinction. This article argues that, while established legal and standards titles should be retained, scholarly and engineering writing should translate security as "anbao", and reserve "anquan" mainly for safety. This is not a cosmetic translation preference, but a proposal for terminological governance in scientific cognition, engineering risk communication and assurance argumentation. The article first surveys the conceptual boundary between safety and security in international and Chinese standards, and analyzes how the current translation overload affects functional safety, SOTIF, information security, cybersecurity, automotive cybersecurity and AI governance. It then uses recent work on AI assurance, safety-security co-assurance and security-informed safety to show why precise terminology is fundamental to scientific arguments that can be examined, challenged and communicated. Finally, it proposes a staged, dual-track writing practice for Chinese technical discourse.

</details>

*Jose Luna,Yankun Wu,Xiaofei Xie,Noa Garcia*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有T2I模型中的性别偏见评估方法碎片化，缺乏统一的测量视角、假设说明和部署上下文解释，限制了技术审计和监管讨论的有效性。

Method: 提出一个三部分组成的审计框架：(1) 基于欧盟AI法案风险类别的用例画像；(2) 整合性别预测、嵌入相似性和下游任务的指标目录；(3) 将上下文相关的伤害类别映射到风险场景的伤害类型学；并引入THUMB卡片作为系统化审计工具。

Result: 构建了一个风险对齐的性别偏见审计框架，提供了THUMB卡片以整合上下文、场景、偏见表现、伤害假设和审计策略。

Abstract: Text-to-image (T2I) generative models are increasingly used to produce content for education, media, and public-facing communication, and are starting to be integrated into higher-impact pipelines. Since generated images tend to reinforce stereotypes, producing representational erasure via "default" depictions and shaping perceptions of who belongs in certain roles, a growing body of work has proposed metrics to quantify gender bias in T2I outputs. Yet existing evaluations remain fragmented. Metrics are often reported without a shared view of what they measure, what assumptions they entail, or how their results should be interpreted under different deployment contexts. This limits the usefulness of gender bias measurement for both technical auditing and emerging governance discussions. We propose a risk-aligned auditing framework for gender bias in T2I models composed of three constituents that connects risk categories, evaluation metrics, and harms. First, we identify risk-tiered use-case profiles aligned with the EU AI Act's risk categories to motivate why auditing expectations may vary with deployment contexts and stakeholder exposure. Second, we construct a metric catalog that consolidates gender-bias evaluation methods and organizes them in three measurement categories: gender prediction, embedding similarity, and downstream task. Third, we introduce a harm typology that maps context-dependent harm categories (e.g., representational, quality-of-service) to specific risk-tired scenarios. Finally, we introduce THUMB cards (Text-to-image Harms-informed Use-case-aligned Metrics of gender Bias) that help formulate auditing systematically by the incorporation of context, scenario and bias manifestation, harm hypotheses, and audit strategy.

</details>

We discuss how perceptions of competence, access to collaborative networks, and competition for limited opportunities shape womens' participation and sense of belonging. As a call to action, we propose community driven discussions, focus groups, and participatory data collection within the ACM womENcourage community to better understand and address these challenges. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AGI已从理论进入政策辩论核心，但关于其时间线、地缘影响及区域准备程度的系统性分析仍然匮乏，尤其缺乏针对欧洲的专门评估。

Abstract: Artificial general intelligence (AGI)--defined here as AI systems that match or exceed humans at most economically useful cognitive work--has moved from speculation to the centre of political and strategic debate. This paper examines three questions: how soon AGI might emerge, how it could reshape geopolitics, and whether Europe is adequately prepared. Drawing on empirical trends in AI capabilities, expert forecasting surveys, and policy analysis, we find that a plausible window for AGI emergence falls between 2030 and 2040, or potentially earlier, though substantial uncertainty remains. Our analysis of the geopolitical implications suggests that AGI could fundamentally alter the global distribution of economic and military power, intensify interstate competition, and strain existing governance frameworks. Assessing Europe's current positioning, we identify critical gaps: limited strategic awareness of frontier AI progress, structural weaknesses in compute infrastructure and talent retention, low rates of industrial AI adoption, and fragmented policy responses at both EU and Member State levels that do not match the potential scale of disruption.These findings point to a need for a coordinated European preparedness agenda. We outline policy options centred on building institutional capacity for AGI situational awareness, strengthening Europe's position in the AI value chain, and developing frameworks for international stability in an era of increasingly capable AI systems.

### [383] [Amplification to Synthesis: A Comparative Analysis of Cognitive Operations Before and After Generative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13785)
*Liz Cho,Dongwook Yoon*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究通过对比2016年和2024年美国大选期间的X平台数据，发现2024年的认知操作模式发生了根本性转变：原创内容从59%飙升至93%，词汇重叠度从0.99骤降至0.27，时间同步性从泛语义协同转向叙事集中共现。这些模式与生成式AI参与的特征高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 认知操作（cognitive operations）在地缘政治领域日益受到关注，生成式AI的兴起可能从根本上改变了这类操作的执行方式，使国家在缺乏适当缓解策略的情况下变得脆弱。此前研究主要关注机器人驱动的放大效应，而对生成式AI带来的新能力缺乏系统分析。

Method: 对比分析2016年和2024年美国大选期间X平台数据集（总计超过13.3万条帖子），采用发帖类型分布、语义聚类、时间同步性分析以及基于Jaccard系数的词汇重叠度测量等四种分析方法。

Result: 2024年数据呈现三种显著变化：原创内容从59%升至93%，转推几乎消失；词汇重叠均值Jaccard分数从0.99降至0.27，帖子围绕相同主题却使用截然不同的表达；时间协调从泛语义同步转向叙事集中的共现模式。

Conclusion: 这些模式指向一种以主动内容生成和叙事特定目标为导向的操作逻辑——与生成式AI介入的特征一致。研究为后续探索生成式AI在认知操作中的作用提供了实证基线，也为安全从业者开发适应后生成式AI威胁环境的检测框架提供了实践参考。

Abstract: Cognitive operations are a rising concern in the geopolitical sphere, a quiet yet rigorous fight for public perception and decision making. While such operations have been extensively studied in the context of bot-driven amplification, the emergence of generative AI introduces a new set of capabilities that may have fundamentally altered how these operations are designed and executed. The possible evolution of cognitive operation via generative AI puts nation states vulnerable without proper mitigation strategies. To address this, we compared behavioral and linguistic coordination patterns in X (formerly Twitter) datasets from the 2016 and 2024 U.S. presidential elections. Utilizing a combined corpus of over 133,000 posts, we applied post-type distribution, semantic clustering, temporal synchrony analysis, and Jaccard-based lexical overlap measures. Findings suggest that the 2024 corpus exhibits a distinct pattern from 2016. Original content rose from 59% to 93% with retweets virtually disappeared; lexical overlap collapsed from a mean Jaccard score of 0.99 to 0.27, with posts converging on the same subject matter expressed in markedly different words; and temporal coordination shifted from pervasive cross-semantic synchrony to narratively concentrated co-occurrence. Taken together, these patterns point toward an operational logic organized around active content generation and narrative-specific targeting - characteristics consistent with generative AI involvement. These findings offer an empirical baseline for future research investigating generative AI's role in the cognitive operation pipeline, and as a practical reference point for security practitioners developing detection frameworks calibrated to the post-generative AI threat environment.

</details>

### [384] [Optimal investment and Pension policy in Pay-As-You-Go systems under forward utility and ageing population](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12698)
*Jennifer Alonso-Garcia,Caroline Hillairet,Sarah Kaakai,Mohamed Mrad*

Main category: q-fin.MF

TL;DR: 本文研究现收现付制（PAYG）养老金体系中引入缓冲基金作为代际风险分担机制的最优投资与养老金政策，采用非零波动率的远期恒定相对风险厌恶（CRRA）效用函数，兼顾可持续性与充足性约束，通过闭式解和数值分析评估不同情景下的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现收现付制养老金体系中，代际风险分担机制存在不足，且传统模型未能同时兼顾可持续性与充足性约束。本文旨在通过引入缓冲基金和前瞻性效用框架，优化投资与养老金政策。

Method: 采用非零波动率的远期CRRA效用函数作为社会规划者的偏好准则，建立包含可持续性与充足性约束的优化模型，推导出最优策略的闭式解，并通过数值模拟分析不同人口、金融和宏观经济情景下的表现。

Result: 得到了最优投资与养老金政策的闭式解，分析了偏好敏感性对养老金方案的影响，数值结果展示了混合PAYG缓冲基金制度在多种情景下的可持续性与充足性。

Conclusion: 该混合PAYG缓冲基金制度能够有效平衡可持续性与充足性，偏好参数对政策设计具有重要影响，数值分析验证了模型在多种情景下的稳健性。

Abstract: This paper investigates optimal investment and pension policies in a Pay-As-You-Go (PAYG) system supplemented by a buffer fund used as an intergenerational risk-sharing mechanism. The social planner's preference criterion is represented by non-zero volatility forward Constant Relative Risk Aversion (CRRA) utilities, and explicitly accounts for both sustainability and adequacy constraints. The optimal policies are characterized in closed form, and an in-depth analysis of the impact of preference sensitivities on the pension scheme is conducted. A detailed numerical analysis is performed to evaluate the sustainability and benefit adequacy of this hybrid PAYG buffer fund arrangement under a range of demographic, financial, and macroeconomic scenarios.

### [385] [Yield Curves Dynamics Using Variational Autoencoders Under No-arbitrage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12764)
*Fusheng Luo,H'elyette Geman*

Main category: q-fin.MF

TL;DR: 本文提出一种物理信息驱动的生成框架，通过在固定收益建模中融合深度学习灵活性与无套利理论约束，解决传统模型在极端宏观环境下的“流形坍塌”和套利违规问题。该框架采用Student-t条件变分自编码器（CVAEsT+LS）提取稳健的厚尾期限结构流形，并由神经随机微分方程（SDE）受无套利偏微分方程（PDE）约束驱动潜在动态演化。在USD、GBP、JPY多主权货币上的实证表明，该方法实现了6.58个基点的平均期限均方根误差，显著优于经典HJM模型，并具备无监督宏观经济体制检测与连续时间情景生成能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准生成模型和未加约束的统计外推在多宏观经济体制下预测期限结构时，会出现"流形坍塌"和严重套利违规；经典HJM模型在极端环境下存在大规模平行漂移和零下限违例问题。深度学习灵活性与固定收益建模严格理论约束之间存在根本性冲突。

Method: 两阶段架构：(1) Student-t条件变分自编码器（CVAEsT+LS）通过动态水平注入提取稳健的厚尾期限结构流形，解耦宏观经济形状动态与绝对基率；(2) 潜在动态演化由连续时间神经随机微分方程（SDE）驱动，并受无套利偏微分方程（PDE）严格约束。

Result: 跨USD/GBP/JPY多主权货币实证：平均期限RMSE达6.58个基点；克服了经典HJM模型在极端环境中的大规模平行漂移和零下限违例；通过相空间向量场分析展示了无监督宏观经济体制检测和连续时间情景生成能力。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个高度可扩展、数学上严谨的期限结构建模演化引擎，成功弥合了深度学习灵活性与固定收益理论约束之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: This paper introduces a physics-informed generative framework that resolves the fundamental conflict between the statistical flexibility of deep learning and the rigorous theoretical constraints of fixed-income modeling. We demonstrate that standard generative models and unconstrained statistical extrapolations suffer from "manifold collapse" and severe arbitrage violations when forecasting term structures across diverse macroeconomic regimes. To overcome this, we propose a two-stage architecture. First, a Student-t Conditional Variational Autoencoder with Dynamic Level Injection (CVAEsT+LS) extracts a robust, heavy-tailed term structure manifold, effectively decoupling macroeconomic shape dynamics from absolute base rates. Second, the latent dynamic evolution is governed by a continuous-time Neural Stochastic Differential Equation (SDE) strictly penalized by a No-Arbitrage Partial Differential Equation (PDE). Empirical results across multiple sovereign currencies (USD, GBP, JPY) confirm that our synergistic approach drastically reduces out-of-sample forecasting errors -- achieving an exceptional 6.58 bps Mean Tenor RMSE -- and successfully overcomes the massive parallel drift and zero-lower-bound violations exhibited by the classical HJM model in extreme environments. Furthermore, through phase space vector field analysis, we demonstrate the model's superior capability in unsupervised macroeconomic regime detection and high-quality continuous-time scenario generation. Ultimately, this research provides a highly scalable, mathematically sound evolutionary engine for term structure modeling.

</details>
